 Ramvilas Sharma with his fiery and provocative essays gave Hindi criticism and review a momentum that could be the dream of any critic
 vah marxvaadi drushti se bhartiya sandarbhon kaa moolyankan karne ke baavjood na keval bhartiya mulyon par karte the, balki apane pathakon ko nirantar bataate rahete the ki bhashaa, sahitya tathaa chintan kii drushti se bharat atyant pracheen or mahaan raashtra he
 He considered Indian history written by the British as a conspiracy
 premchand, bhaaratendu or niraala ke sahitya par adbhut kaam ke saath hi unhone bhashaa, sahitya, sanskrit or samaaj par kaam kiya tha
 He said that if we want to evaluate the history of India correctly, then we have to study our ancient texts
 angrejon ne jaan-boojhkar bhartiya itihaas ko nasht kiya he
 Only by doing this they could rule this great nation
 bharat main vyaapt jati, dharm ke algaav kaa jitna gaharaa prakatikaran angrejon ke aane ke baad hota he, utana gaharaa prabhaav pehle ke itihaas main maujuud nahin he
 Only by dividing the society, the British could rule this great nation and they have done the same
 itihaas kii samasyaon se jujhna maano dow
 Ramvilas Sharma had his first and last vows
 isiilie vah jeevanabhar bhartiya itihaas kii har samasya kaa nidaan khojane main jute rahe
 He was opposed when he said that Aryans are native to India
 unhone kaha ki arya pashchim asia yaa kisi duusare sthaan se bharat main nahin aae hai, balki sach yah he ki ve bharat se pashchim asia kii ore gaye hai
 Dr
 ram vilaas sharma ne likhaa tha, ‚Äò‚Äòduusari sahastrabdi isa purv bade-bade jan abhiyaanon kii sahastrabdi he
 Meanwhile, Indian Aryan contingents spread from Iraq to Turkey
 ve apni bhashaa or samskruti kii chhap sarvatra chhodte jate hai
 The capitalist historians have shed the opposite Ganges
 jo yug aaryon ke bahirgaman kaa he, use ve bharat main unke pravesh kaa yug kehete hai
 At the same time, they try to make the present residents of West Asia lose the aspect of their ancient culture, which is related to India
 sabase pehle swayan bharatvasiyon ko yah sambandh samajhnaa he, phir use apane padosiyon ko samajhaana he
 The present social system that is hungry, illiteracy, superstition and new diseases has to be changed
 iske liye bharat or uske padosiyon kaa sammilit prayaas aavashyak he
 Whenever this effort takes place, it is imperative that our current relations with our neighbors will change and with them changing, they and we will recognize our old relations anew
 ateet kaa vaigyanik, vastuparak vivechan vartmaan samaaj ke punargathan ke prashn se judaa hua he
 "- [west Asia and Rigveda book, page no
 20] In the research work done by Ramvilas Sharma on the prevalence of Indian culture in West Asia and Europe, he resorted to dance, history, philology
 shabdon kii sanrachana or unki utpatti kaa vishleshan kar ve is nishkarsh par pahonchte hai ki aaryon kii bhashaa kaa gaharaa prabhaav europe or pashchim asia kii bhashaaon par he
 He argued that in the context of progress, tradition is a fundamental value, whether it is placed in the context of literature or society
 duusare shabdon main bina saahitiyik parampara ko samajhe na to pragatisheel aalochana or sahitya kii rachana ho sakati he or na hi apni aitihaasik parampara se alag rahakar koi bada saamaajik badlaav sambhav he
 But what is useful and meaningful in tradition cannot be adopted without evaluating it
 sahitya ajtak main aaj ham ramvilas sharma kii punyatithi par unki aalochana pustak 'parampara kaa moolyankan' se ek ansh de rahe
 This book is a byproduct of his inventive, useful vision and meaningful search on tradition
 suvikhyath samalochak dow ramvilas sharma ne is pustak main jahaan hindi jati ke saanskrithik itihaas kii ruparekha prastut kii he, vahiin apane-apane yug main vishisht bhawabhooti or tulsi kii lokabhimukh kavy-chetana kaa vistrut moolyankan bhi kiya he
 *** Book excerpt: Evaluation of the tradition- Ram Vilas Sharmasachthya is related to the entire life of man
 aarthik jivan ke alaava manushya ek praani ke rup main bhi apana jivan bitaata he
 In literature, many of his primitive feelings result, which connect him to the last
 is baat ko baar-baar kehane main koi haani nahin he ki sahitya vichaardhaara maatr nahin he
 In it, the sense of man, his feelings, internal motivations are also expressed
 sahitya kaa yah paksh apekshaakrit sthaayee hota he
 At the time historical materialism was established, evolutionism was dominated by biology
 yah vikaswad sahi ho chaahe galat, yah baat sach he ki sahitya main vikaas-prakriya usee tarah sampann nahin hoti jaise samaaj main
 In the course of social development, capitalist civilization can be called more progressive than feudal civilization and socialist civilization than capitalist civilization
 puraane charakhe or karghe ke mukaable mashiinon ke vyavhaar se shram kii utpaadakta bahut bad gayi he
 But it is not necessary that the future of capitalist society should be better than the poet of feudal society
 yah bhi sambhav he ki aadhunik sabhyataa kaa vikaas kavita ke vikaas kaa virdohi ho or kavi swayan bikaoo maal ban rahaa ho
 In practice it is seen that the poets of the 19th and 20th centuries - whether in India and in Europe - are being recognized by the old poets and when they reach around them, they consider themselves blessed
 ye jo tamaam kavi apane purvavarti kaviyon kii rachanaaon kaa manan karte hai, ye unka anukaran nahin karte, unase sikhte hai, or swayan nayi paramparaon ko janm dete hai
 The literature which is written by copying others, is of inferior quality and is indicative of cultural inability
 jo mahan sahityakar hai, unki kala kii aavriti nahin ho sakati, yahan tak ki ek bhashaa se duusari bhashaa main anuwaad karne par unka kalatmak soundarya jyon kaa-tyon nahi bana rahata
 This is a big difference between industrial production and artistic production
 america ne atum bam banaaya, rus ne bhi banaaya par shakespeare ke naatako jaisi cheez kaa utpaadan dubaara england main bhi nahin hua
 Materialism is of two types, a mechanical materialism, this dialectical materialism
 yantrik bhautikwaad kii visheshta yah he ki vah chetana ko aarthik sambandhon kaa pratibimb maatr maanata he
 The image is mechanical
 jab chetana pratibimb he, tab samskruti bhi pratibimb he, sahitya bhi pratibimb he
 In this situation, the culture of the culture also changes completely if the old economic structure is changed
 is yantrik bhautikwaad kaa vikaas france main hua; 19ve sadi main jab bhautik vigyaan kaa vikaas hua, to is vigyaan kaa darshanik drushtikon isi yantric bhautikwaad se prabhavit hua
 In contrast, dialectical materialism recognizes the relative independence of human beings by considering their consciousness as an influence on economic relations
 aarthik sambandhon se prabhavit hona ek baat he, unke dwaara chetana kaa nirdhaarit hona or baat he
 Materialism does not mean fate
 sab kuch paristhitiyon dwaara anivaaryat: nirdhaarit nahin ho jaataa
 If man is not the regulator of circumstances, then circumstances are also not the regulator of man
 donon kaa sambandh dwandvatmak he
 This is why literature is inherently independent
 gulaami america main thi or gulaami athens main thi kintu athens kii sabhyataa ne saare europe ko prabhavit kiya or gulaamon ke america maalikon ne maanav samskruti ko kuch bhi nahin diya
 Feudalism persisted throughout the world, but in this feudal world there were only two centers of great poetry - India and Iran
 poonjivadi vikaas europe ke tamaam deshon main hua par refail, leonardo da vinci or micel angelo italy kii dein hai
 Here we see that on the one hand it is possible to develop art under special social conditions, on the other hand we also see that even if there are equal social conditions, there is no equal development of art
 yahaan ham asaadhaaran pratibhashali manushya kii adwitiya bhoomika bhi dekhte hai
 Just as socialization of industrial production takes place in the capitalist system, socialization of literary work does not happen
 kaarkaane main 1500 majdoor din- pratidin thaan ke thaan kapade nikaalte hai
 If the litterateurs are admitted to the literature making factory, then they may be overcome some of their faults, or they may fight each other so much that they do not get free time for any work, but regular high quality novels , Poetry, drama, according to the five-year plan, will continue to be removed from that factory, it is less likely
 sahityakar aapasi sahyog se laabh uthaate hai par abhi tak us takanic kaa pataa nahin lagaaya ja sakaa, jise logon ko sikhaakar sahitya kaa samuhik utpaadan kiya ja sake
